          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">everyone</span></div>

        


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a href="/review/list/666003-silvana?shelf=military-espionage" class="actionLinkLite">military-espionage</a>, 
              <a href="/review/list/666003-silvana?shelf=top-20" class="actionLinkLite">top-20</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer10076775">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2864857853378131988">“Somewhere under the Atlantic, a Soviet sub commander has just made a fateful decision. The Red October is heading West. The Americans want her. The Soviet want her back. And the most incredible chase in history is on….”<br /><br />Ah, one of my favorite authors of all time. The incredible Mr. Clancy. I loveee political-military-espionage-techno-thrillers! And Clancy is definitely the man for it. I’ve fallen in love with his works since years ago, been collecting them, until now he sells more books to me co</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText2864857853378131988">“Somewhere under the Atlantic, a Soviet sub commander has just made a fateful decision. The Red October is heading West. The Americans want her. The Soviet want her back. And the most incredible chase in history is on….”<br /><br />Ah, one of my favorite authors of all time. The incredible Mr. Clancy. I loveee political-military-espionage-techno-thrillers! And Clancy is definitely the man for it. I’ve fallen in love with his works since years ago, been collecting them, until now he sells more books to me compared with other authors. Well, except Enid Blyton.<br /><br />The Hunt for Red October is his first novel, published in 1984 (I wish I could read when I was three). It is also deemed by many as one of his best works. I fully concur.<br /><br />The plot is magnificently built, the characters (besides the famous Jack Ryan) are awesome, the accuracy is so genuinely believable, and what I like most is perhaps the submarine warfare and all those stuffs. (FYI, Das Boot is one of my all time fave war movies).<br /><br />“Conn, sonar, the enemy bearing is one-nine-two.”<br />“Preparing to fire. Flooding tubes. Outer torpedo tube doors are open.”<br />“Recheck firing solution!”<br />“Torpedoes in the water port side!”<br />“Left full rudder! Prepare countermeasures!”<br />“Brace for impact!”<br /><br />HELL YEAH!<br />Totally riveting! Breathlessly exhilarating! I bet you’ll find difficulties to put it down.<br /><br />PS: The movie (starring Sean Connery and Alec Baldwin) is kinda good. But I still recommend the real thing, since it’s far more complex and exciting.</span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/1058425061?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Sep 18, 2014</a>

      <a href="/user/show/301807-donna" class="user" title="Donna">Donna</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it">really liked it</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span></span>

          <a href="/book/show/1001555.The_Hunt_for_Red_October" title="Hardcover 9780870212857" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a href="/review/list/301807-donna?shelf=crime" class="actionLinkLite">crime</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer1058425061">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5770085798134190733">I was about 65% through this book when I picked it up for a bedtime read. Next thing I knew it was 2:45 a.m. Not wanting to put it down, but knowing I had plans for the morning, I turned off my light and tried to sleep..."tried" being the operative word. Thirty minutes later I was still wide awake and could feel the adrenaline still pumping through me. <br /><br />Although the book is set in the mid-1980s and concerns the U.S. and the Russians chasing a Soviet submarine, given today's world and current Russ</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText5770085798134190733">I was about 65% through this book when I picked it up for a bedtime read. Next thing I knew it was 2:45 a.m. Not wanting to put it down, but knowing I had plans for the morning, I turned off my light and tried to sleep..."tried" being the operative word. Thirty minutes later I was still wide awake and could feel the adrenaline still pumping through me. <br /><br />Although the book is set in the mid-1980s and concerns the U.S. and the Russians chasing a Soviet submarine, given today's world and current Russian aggressiveness it's not too far from reality. There is, however, a good deal of technical jargon which I just skimmed over -- it sets the mood but is not necessary to understand what is going on. <br /><br />I enjoyed this book very much. But once you are past half-way, don't read it at bedtime.</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="5770085798134190733">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked &amp;&amp; exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&amp;name=' + shelf_name + '&amp;a=' + action + '&amp;authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('2dCbSgRVz2++86gvpZcA0yk+3tRVh3UHgP10uBS7ZcW8BKSZ9ofblTIr3JTb9uZhYMkdzRxaMq3q9HEq2C6TgA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&amp;book_id=' + book_id + '&amp;refresh=true' + '&amp;authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('MgUSH1jp+x3uwZWrtf9NcYBLywDU4z3v1FHJRo7a8ZBX0S3Mqjvv52IZ4RDLnqvDybwIGZ0+ekW+WMzUQk8H1Q==')})

    <div class=" clearFloats bigBox" id="aboutAuthor"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/3892.Tom_Clancy">About Tom Clancy</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
      <a href="/author/show/3892.Tom_Clancy"><img alt="3892" src="http://d.gr-assets.com/authors/1407672935p2/3892.jpg" class="right" /></a>
    <div class="readable">
      
<span id="freeTextContainer13612108788724293291">Tom Clancy was an English major at Baltimore’s Loyola College. As a Maryland insurance broker with a passion for naval history, his dream of writing a novel came true with his first effort, <em>The Hunt for Red October</em> (1984). <br /><br />He since wrote more than a dozen novels, which have a blend of realism and authenticity, intricate plotting, and razor-sharp suspense. Ten of the novels, including <em>The Teeth of</em></span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText13612108788724293291">Tom Clancy was an English major at Baltimore’s Loyola College. As a Maryland insurance broker with a passion for naval history, his dream of writing a novel came true with his first effort, <em>The Hunt for Red October</em> (1984). <br /><br />He since wrote more than a dozen novels, which have a blend of realism and authenticity, intricate plotting, and razor-sharp suspense. Ten of the novels, including <em>The Teeth of the Tiger</em> (Berkley, 2004), feature the character Jack Ryan, former stock broker and CIA employee. <br /><br />Clancy’s non-fiction works include a series of guided tours of America’s warfighting assets, Submarine, Armored Cav, Fighter Wing, Marine, and Airborne.<br /><br />He lived in Maryland.<br /><br />The following are the books and approximate time frame in the <em>Jack Ryan Universe</em><br /><br />Without Remorse		1969-73<br />Patriot Games			1981-82<br />Red Rabbit			1982<br />The Hunt for Red October	1984<br />The Cardinal of the Kremlin	1986<br />Clear and Present Danger	1988<br />The Sum of All Fears		1990-91<br />Debt of Honor			1995-96<br />Executive Orders		1996<br />Rainbow Six			1999-2000<br />The Bear and the Dragon	2002<br />The Teeth of the Tiger	2006<br />Dead or Alive			2007<br />Locked On			2007<br />Threat Vector			2009<br />Command Authority		2013<br />Support and Defend		2014<br />Full Force and Effect		2014</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="13612108788724293291">...more</a>

    </div>
    <a href="/author/show/3892.Tom_Clancy" class="actionLink moreLink">More about Tom Clancy...</a>
